</div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-6"><likes-rating :perfume_id="25967" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></likes-rating></div><div class="cell small-6"><seasons-rating :perfume_id="25967" chart="show" type-chart="small-chart" colors="retro"></seasons-rating></div><div class="small-12 medium-6 text-center" style="max-height: 50px"><div itemprop="aggregateRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/AggregateRating" itemscope><p class="info-note">Perfume rating&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingValue">4.42</span>&nbsp;out of&nbsp;<span itemprop="bestRating">5</span> with&nbsp;<span itemprop="ratingCount" content="14681">14,681</span> votes<meta itemprop="reviewCount" content="1544"/></p></div></div></div><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell small-12" itemprop="description" v-pre><p><b>Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum</b> by <b>Chanel</b> is a Woody Aromatic fragrance for men. <b>Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum</b> was launched in 2014. The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Polge. Top notes are Grapefruit, Lemon, Mint, Pink Pepper, Bergamot, Aldehydes and Coriander; middle notes are Ginger, Nutmeg, Jasmine and Melon; base notes are Incense, Amber, Cedar, Sandalwood, Patchouli, Amberwood and Labdanum. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Bleu de Chanel is a sophisticated and contemporary fragrance from Chanel that hit the market in 2010. Chanel introduces its enhanced version, Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum, in summer of  2014. The fragrance is dedicated to freedom—endless, deep and boundless. 
</p>

<p>
The woody-aromatic composition created by Jacques Polge follows the original path but goes down into a sensual and oriental amber territory. Wood maintains the freshness of the original in this variant, enriched with depth and velvet amber woods. 
</p>

<p>
The fragrance is available as 50 and 100 ml Eau de Parfum.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a     <div class="strike-title"><span>All Reviews By Date</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
        <div class="cell destinationreview"></div>                    <div id="parent2324842" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2324842" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="AJ Amit"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2185321"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="AJ Amit" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25967.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum"title="Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2324842ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2324842" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2185321">AJ Amit</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-23"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729694343" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The opening is very citrusy of lemon, bergamote and grapefruit along with woody and ambery notes.<br />
<br />
It is not spicy and bold as the dior sauvage but it is rich body lotion kind of fresh fragrance. It is timeless and very versatile which is great for the beginners.<br />
<br />
Longevity is only 5-6 hour with 7-8 sprays on me along with moderate projection of 1 hour so it is not a wonderfully performer to justify its price. It is very silent fresh fragrance. BDC is not my favourite one but I like to wear sometimes.<br />
<br />
Rating:<br />
Scent - 9/10<br />
Longevity - 7/10<br />
Projection - 6/10<br />
Price - 5/10 (higher based on performance)<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2073655">austinmdpedi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-12">10/12/24 22:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>BDC would likely be my go to if I could only have one fragrance. About 10 years ago I read an Esquire article and bought Aventus. It was my first fragrance purchase in 20+ years… since my 20s.  I wore it occasionally from age 45-50, always eliciting strong and generally favorable comments. A few years ago, I decided I wanted a second fragrance (perhaps something a bit more subtle and versatile) and BDC is what I chose. It boosted my desire to dive headlong into this world so I’m appreciative of it. It is truly a wonderful year round, any season, day or night scent. If I’m asked for a fragrance recommendation from someone that I know has zero interest in trying several, this has never let me down. The ultimate safe blind buy. The perfect gift fragrance.  It is great for work, isn’t overpowering at the office but is pleasant and will be noticed. It’s a great date night choice.  You can wear it to a wedding. You can wear it to a ballgame.  Your lumberjack friends will just think you smell good. You will spend enough that it feels special.  The scent itself is basically high quality citrus and sandalwood. Lovely scent. Easy. Clean. <br />
Lemony opening. Bergamot (Spicy, slightly bitter orange). Mid is more floral. Lavender. <br />
Dry down fantastic. Woody. Less spicy than Aventus.  Less sillage and length too than Aventus. <br />
If I apply more liberally (6 sprays) I’ll get an easy 8+ hours with solid projection for half of that.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2313940"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2313940#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2312768" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I own the Parfum version which is a slightly denser than the EDP.<br />
<br />
The EDP is very elegant, and suitable for anything: day, night, dumb reach, work, gym, date, church, wedding, baptism, divorce, you name it (see what I did there?), <br />
It will make you feel clean, fresh, and polish.<br />
<br />
No clone gets even closer to the sole of BdC EDP shoes, metaphorically speaking.<br />
It’s better than niche fragrances? No, but those come with some wrinkles (not versatile, challenging, rarely available to test, etc).<br />
<br />
I am not going to describe the scent. There are tons of comments and reviews, but to me, this is a signature scent worthy.<br />
<br />
I wish longevity and projection would be better, but I have a 150ml that I can just go to town spraying and not care at all. It will not offend anyone.<br />
<br />
And that’s it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2305895"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2305895#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305195" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2300402"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2300402#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2299444" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2299444" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EvanGiorgioArmani"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2258882"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2258882.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EvanGiorgioArmani" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2299444ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2299444" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2258882">EvanGiorgioArmani</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-29">09/29/24 18:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Simplicity and elegance in a bottle. For those who say this is generic - sure, but it's also complex and smells very luxurious and professional. Coming from someone who owns and loves Sauvage Parfum, this is on another level when it comes to a simple smelling, clean fragrance experience. To me, this is Bleu de Chanel EDP is the KING of blue fragrances. I have smelled the edt version, although I liked it, it was just not complex enough and not enough depth that I know and love in the edp version. I have not yet tried the parfum version, but I bet it smells very nice too. The edp just gives me everything I could possibly want, even when I cannot decide what to wear. <br />
<br />
The EDP is bright, sparkly, slightly nutty (from the nutmeg listed I would guess), woody, a little ambery, and piney (from the ginger). I love the ginger note in this fragrance, it is a very underrated element to this fragrance composition. Furthermore, there is a floral presence that I always get, and that has to be coming from the jasmine...so good. <br />
Professional, sexy, versatile, and simply elegant. Wear this anytime, anywhere. <br />
<br />
8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2299444"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2299444#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2298833" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1290480">soumbanerjee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-29">09/29/24 06:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Make no mistake, none of the clones smell more than 80% of what the original smells. This is one of the rare ones where I wore the clones before wearing the original. This smells rich, blue citrusy with copious amount of incense and amber in it. May be the clones mimic the EDT more and not this EDP and hence I feel this difference.<br />
<br />
Classy smell, easy 10+ hours on clothes before becoming closer to skin (which for a blue category fragrance is damn good IMHO). Since I haven't used the older batches cannot compare whether the longevity has reduced due to reformulation over the years or not but yes moderate silage for sure. Overall a perfect all weather perfume.<br />
<br />
PS - There is a lot of comparisons by frag heads on this vs. Versace Dylan blue. I love this and cannot stand Dylan Blue and the only reason is Dylan Blue feels nauseatingly ambroxan/amber heavy compared to this.<br />
<br />
Still feel YSL Y EDP is a winner in the blue category all weather fragrances at least to me (after having used Sauvage, Y, BDC and Dylan Blue).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
One of the GOAT's.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2289222"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2289222#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288280" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2218044">SimpleMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-19">09/19/24 10:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was the first Bleu de Chanel that I tried out of the line (Given only this and the EDT were out at the time) and it is personally my favorite I do find the Parfum a bit more darker and a great addition to the line and this one brighter but it rides the line perfectly between the EDT and the Partum IMO. (Side Note: Chanel anytime you wanna drop the elixir we're ready). The EDP has slightly more depth than the EDT and I like the touch of incense in both of them that I feel the Parfum is missing. Probably the most versatile blue fragrance I have ever owned and with it being the first one I picked up from the line almost 9 years ago I will always have a place for this in my collection. Even this far down the line no matter what anyone else feels I don't think this is overplayed or boring yes its not the most exciting thing out there but damn its good. <br />
<br />
My personal Ratings<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10 (8+ hour range)<br />
Projection: 7.75/10 (just beyond arms length for 2-3 feet for most of its life with loud projection for the first 1-1.5 hours)<br />
Price: 7.5/10 (For what you get its totally worth it)<br />
Overall: 8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2288280"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2288280#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2287065" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Is it a "niche" work of art or a statement piece? No, let's not kid ourselves, it's pretty much engineered to be as inoffensive as possible, but it's one of those scents that remind you that wearing a fragrance is not necessarily about what you want to smell, but what you want to smell like. <br />

I'd probably go for the more sparkly EDT for summertime but I like how this is slightly toned down and more ambery so it's better for the rest of the year.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2215083">blockwash</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-08">08/08/24 03:33</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bleu de Chanel EDP is one of the greatest fragrances of all time. It is a timeless scent that is mass appealing. I hear a lot about how generic this fragrance is, as well as how overused it is. This fragrance is popular for a reason, it has a sophisticated clean shower-gel type of scent. It is sweet and woody as well as fresh and creamy. I like to think it has an 'old money' vibe to it that not a lot of blue fragrances have.<br />
The performance of BDC EDP could be better. With a normal number of sprays, I get 5-6 hours when applied to skin. On clothes it's about 6-8. If over sprayed you will be smelling this for a whole workday, 8 hrs. The projection could also be better here, the scent bubble reduces drastically as the day goes on.<br />
The bottle presentation is simplistic and appealing. The magnetic cap is an added bonus, I am appreciative of the cap's quality. I think the worst part about BDC EDP is the atomizer. It is just okay. For the price that BDC EDP goes for I would expect a crisp consistent atomizer, but what I got was an atomizer that sprays inconsistently.<br />
BDC EDP is a very versatile fragrance. You can dress it up, down, and all around. I have been complimented at the office, out with the boys, dates, parties, and concerts with BDC EDP. This fragrance can be worn in all seasons and times of day, but I think it particularly shines in warmer seasons in the evening.<br />
<br />
I don't like to rate out of 10, but I will just to summarize the fragrance.<br />
<br />
7.5/10 hands down. Beautiful and masculine 'old money' fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2242482"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2242482#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2240076" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1661620">copenhagenfragrence</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-05">08/05/24 08:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review of Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum 100 ml in 2024. Batch code 9236.<br />
<br />
My first BDC, and I must say that it smells very nice, but it DOES NOT LAST LONG ENOUGH... Especially at this price point. My Ralph Lauren Polo Blue Eau de Parfum lasts 6-8 hours, but this lasts only 4-5 hours at almost double the price... How is this even possible at this price point? <br />
<br />
This is my first Chanel perfume, and I am disappointed. The smell is very good and "blue" with a bit of complexity to it, and I like that. But the performance is completely unacceptable. <br />
<br />
Like do Chanel not know that this will be an "office fragrance"? Then why not make it last 8 hours as an Eau de Parfum? Obviously they have cheaped out with the oil concentration. <br />
<br />
Get a grip Chanel! You sell a mediocre product at a premium price point. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137868">EmilZakaryan924</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-28">07/28/24 20:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I went to the Chanel boutique today and tried some of their mens fragrances.<br />
<br />
This is a modern masterpiece. Probably one of the most versatile fragrance I have ever smelt. Not as dark and woody like the Parfum, and not as fresh as the EDT. This is perfectly in the middle and my personal favorite from the Bleu de Chanel line. BDC Eau de Parfum starts off very amber-y, citrusy, woody, and a bit fresh. It dries down to a more woody and amber-y version of the opening. This is the absolute best fragrance for the office because it is so professional, sophisticated, and classy. This is an absolutely beautiful fragrance that is one of my favorites from Chanel, excluding some from the Allure Homme lineup. <br />
<br />
Let's talk about performance. I get around 7-8 hours on my skin with a medium projection leaning masculine. Since this is so versatile, you can wear this year round, day and night, dressed up in a suit, dressed down casually, and overall as an everyday fragrance for school or the office. I recommend this fragrance for all age groups since it is so beautiful and versatile. This has a good and comparable versatility to that of Dior Sauvage Eau de Parfum. <br />
<br />
Lastly, is it a safe blind buy? Hell yeah it is. If you love amber-y, citrusy, professional fragrances then you will absolutely love this. <br />
<br />
In conclusion:<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Projection: 7.5/10<br />
Versatility: 10/10<br />
<br />
Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum: 10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2232276"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2232276#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2231254" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This kicked off the blue fragrance revolution.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2224280"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2224280#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2224197" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; More sprays equals more alcohol physically on your skin, allowing it to project longer which results in increased longevity. I've sprayed this ~4 times on multiple occasions and it lasts about 4-5 hours. When I spray this stuff 6+ times it lasts most of the day on my skin because of the increased volume. My girlfriend also noticed the differences in projection and longevity when I applied it more. <br />

Chanel is a rarity in that it does not constantly churn out new releases and that is something that I like and respect but if you are going to take that approach you also need to ensure that your existing catalogue is the best it can be in every area including projection, sillage and longevity. <br />

Compliment MONSTER, although there are a lot of blue/fresh/ambroxan fragrances right now, this is still the classiest and probably the best IMO. <br />
<br />
Smell : 10/10<br />
Performance: 7/10<br />
Price : 5/10<br />
<br />
Absolutely worth getting if you have the money, if not there are a ton of alternatives.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2206877"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2206877#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2205309" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2202678" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="patsnotmyname"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138496"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="patsnotmyname" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2202678ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2202678" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2138496">patsnotmyname</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-28">06/28/24 23:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This fragrance is losing credibility in being one of the best men's fragrances. It is the best "dumb reach" of all time, but don't let that stop you from admiring its masterful blend. This is still a very UNIQUE fragrance even in the sea of blue, shower gel perfumery; I believe that this stuff is not overused. I've had this as a signature since the beginning of the year and I never get bored of it.<br />
As I've gotten more into fragrances, I literally have not tested a fragrance that smells better than this. I understand the fact that this is a common fragrance and I've been trying to explore for another signature and I've smelled a lot of new things, but no fragrance does it like this. <br />
<br />
Anyway, my review:<br />
<br />
2-3 SPRAYS:<br />
I would go 2 sprays on lower neck and one either on clothes or back of neck for office/school or casual, respectively. You genuinely don't need more. Don't listen to the "you need to overspray" sentiment. Another thing to note about this fragrance is that it's fairly mature so if you want to wear this and you want it to suit you, dress well.<br />
<br />
Longevity: 10 hours<br />
As for all perfumes, olfactory fatigue is commonplace, but don't be fooled, it stays with you practically the whole day. It's the later stage notes that you don't notice that are still there (actually the best part of the fragrance) that make it feel like it has no longevity but I promise you, it does.<br />
<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Pros - When I got this fragrance the citrus at the top was too strong but after letting it maturate it became less harsh. The middle and bottom stages are indescribably good, I'm not really sure what I like most, it might just be how every note compliments each other. It creates a perfect scent bubble that isn't just a non-existent skin scent but also not a beast mode.<br />
<br />
Cons - i've come back to edit my comment: the citrus is no longer aggressive, it just needed time to maturate. My other point, however, still stands: this is for an older, more sophisticated man, and I'm a teen, so it doesn't suit me too well.<br />
<br />
TLDR: this fragrance is essentially perfect and I see nothing bad about it</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2202678"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2202678#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2202677" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2198225" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="PaulRDE"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2174552"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="PaulRDE" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2198225ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2198225" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2174552">PaulRDE</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-24">06/24/24 12:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was the first fragrance I ever purchased, back in early 2023. Before making my choice, I compared a bunch of different summer scents—when I say a lot, I mean over 15 different perfumes. I tested each one on my skin, waited several hours to assess their lasting power and appeal, and ultimately decided on Bleu De Chanel EDP. I was catched by its citrus-fresh aroma.<br />
<br />
Now, as my 150ml bottle is nearly empty, I feel equipped to provide a thorough review. Unfortunately, my initial love for this scent has faded. For reasons I can't quite pinpoint, the fragrance now seems dull and occasionally even irritating to me. Maybe it's a case of overuse, I don't know.<br />
<br />
In terms of longevity, Bleu De Chanel EDP performs adequately. However, its projection on my skin is disappointing. This morning, before school, I applied it generously—on my arms, neck, and other areas, totaling around 10 sprays. I also reapplied it every two hours. Yet, when I asked a friend if he could still detect the scent 45 minutes after reapplication, he said he couldn't, unless he was extremely close to my neck, within 10 centimeters.<br />
<br />
In conclusion, while Bleu De Chanel EDP initially impressed me with its fresh and vibrant notes, its lack of lasting projection and the eventual waning of its appeal have led to a less favorable experience over time. I wouldn't buy it again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2198225"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2198225#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2197944" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Projection: 7.5/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Compliment factor: 9.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2185648"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2185648#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2185355" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2057464">Mattynice74</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-11">06/11/24 17:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The amount of people hating on this fragrance is insane to me. <br />
<br />
Bleu is a masterpiece. It simply is, and it's why all these other houses started making BLUE fragrances. There is a reason for that,  houses try and dip into that pool, just like all the Aventus type frags, and BR540, etc etc. Because this DNA started an entire genre of fragrances. <br />
<br />
Not every fragrance has to be polarizing. If you want polarizing, go invest in Montale. If you want a clean, fresh, classy, everyday scent, with with depth that smells finished, then buy BdC.<br />
<br />
I own over 100 fragrances, and this gets much more wear than many of my niche stuff. It's mass appealing, most women do love it, it works in any situation, in any season, and nobody will be choked out by all the vanilla that every guy wears today.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Not sure why it doesn't seem to perform for others the way it does for me, but I suppose that just means more for me. My skin usually just drinks up fragrances like it found an oasis after walking the desert for days, but this has some staying power for me, and I still get compliments many hours after application. <br />
It's classy and bleu!! Maybe a bit overplayed, but I can't see this getting "old" for me anytime soon. If you want to seem like you've got your shit together, just spray this on, and do a half decent job putting together a coordinated outfit, then you're golden. Nobody is gonna hate on this, and 99 percent of people are gonna LOVE the way you smell. Only the fragrance "community" is gonna see this as played out, and if you live in BFE Ohio,  like myself, then most other men aren't gonna be wearing this; and most men around you probably aren't wearing any type of fragrance at all for that matter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2001024">punkb0nes</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-05">06/05/24 13:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It may be basic, but it sets the standard for a reason. This stuff is super safe and mass-appealing, citrus, smoky, woody, clean. The opening is very grapefruit forward, and in the dry down I get PDM Percival vibes (another favorite of mine). Not super long lasting or loud, but it's not meant to be nuclear. Would like to see how it compares to the rest in the line</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2179101"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2179101#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2178841" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2178841" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="danilodeathayde"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1620729"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1620729.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="danilodeathayde" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2178841ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2178841" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1620729">danilodeathayde</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-05">06/05/24 10:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>(I notice it's more common for me to be disappointed with tests I conduct through decants ordered from specialized stores than with brand flaconettes or by testing directly from the bottle in stores. I wonder if there's something to that, as I've ordered several times from the two most specialized stores in this field and have an unusually high amount of disappointment with generic scents of very low longevity and projection.)<br />
<br />
I test the parfum along with the EDP, using decants, and find them both so weak and close to the skin that after ten minutes, I generously reapply each on my arms and olfactory strips. Both are pleasant, citrusy, and fresh, with the Parfum showing much more incense in the opening. Even the Parfum is much more light-citrus-green-blue than woody, contrary to the listed notes. The woody aspect, to my nose, is just a base of Iso E Super and a bit of sandalwood with its smoothness. At first, I notice a bit more incense in the Parfum, which makes it more interesting than the EDP, but both have a very generic-pleasant vibe. It reminds me of Tommy Now, but less fresh, with a slightly more sophisticated air with its incense and sandalwood and costing ten times more. It also reminds me of Polo Blue and other citrusy blue fragrances, but less blue than those (perhaps it's more of a green than blue fragrance) and more on the slightly woody citrus side, but without the earthy depth and roots of something like Terre d'Hermès.<br />
<br />
Soon, the EDP practically disappears from my skin, while the Parfum remains, though timidly. This contrast is stark as I test it alongside Nuit d'Issey EDP and Malbec Noir (an EDT), both with a similarly citrusy, fruity, woody, and incense profile, and these project and are much more noticeable from opening to dry down.<br />
<br />
Going on for more than half an hour after application, the Parfum begins to redeem itself a bit. The hedione becomes more present, with its characteristic non-astringent cleanliness, and the citrus and fruity notes differentiate more, maintaining a certain creaminess (a creaminess I also identify in another Chanel, like Allure Edition Blanche). The EDP, on the other hand, appears dull, bland, and without distinguishable personality.<br />
<br />
**************************************************************************<br />
<br />
In short, it's a perfume to consider if you're looking for something that doesn't offend and doesn't stand out for any particular feature but also wants to convey status and spend ten times more than you should on a perfume. But, in fact, if that's what you're looking for and money is no issue, spend a bit more and get the Parfum, which is considerably better.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2177171"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2177171#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172235" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2172235" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="BMulroney"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137435"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2137435.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="BMulroney" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.25967.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum"title="Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2172235ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2172235" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137435">BMulroney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 05:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bleu de Chanel is a masterpiece of constraint, balance and quiet luxurious confidence.  The blend of notes within this superlative fragrance are so harmonious that this is not a scent that shouts loudly or waves it's arms around to get your attention. Instead, it quietly gets on with the job of being a beautiful men's fragrance suitable for any setting.  <br />
<br />
The citrus and aldehyde top notes remain part of the overall flavour as the parfum develops, without ever dominating or becoming too sharp.  There is a hint of sweetness that is never cloying and the woody, spicy notes linger in the background adding depth and warmth.  <br />
<br />
The biggest strength of Blue de Chanel is it is applicable for any man in any situation.  I feel comfortable wearing this in jeans and a t-shirt, or wearing a bespoke suit.  When wearing it the smell conveys the sense of being clean, well groomed and confident.  Although a "blue" fragrance there is more than sufficient depth to be wearable all year around, making it an easy "signature" that I can reach for at all times.  <br />
<br />
Whenever I wear Bleu de Chanel I enjoy the smell at all stages of it's development, giving me confidence in what others around experience.<br />
<br />
For all of the praise that I, and many others, have for Bleu de Chanel it should be pointed out what it doesn't deliver.  If I want a spicier, sexier fragrance that combines heavier notes with greater projection then this is not for you.  There are times when I want those things and will turn to Penhaligon's Halfeti, Boss Bottled Elixir, Lalique Encre Noir, Tom Ford Noir etc to get the qualities that Bleu de Chanel does not provide.<br />
<br />
If, however, you want a clean, fresh smelling man's fragrance with depth and substance then Bleu de Chanel is beyond reproach and is, in my opinion, the best designer fragrance of it's type.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2114601">NauticaVoyageFan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-20">05/20/24 17:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Bleu De Chanel by Chanel is basically your average summer fragrance which is saved by its good bergamot and mint notes yet this is very overused with many other options that are not only better but also less used it isn't really recommended to add to your collection. it is very bland and simple so don't expect anything big from this fragrance as it lacks anything that makes it stand out and the similarities with Versace Eros make it even more unlikely that you will stand out with this.<br />
<br />
The fragrance has decent longevity so expect it to be able to last a full day out, especially on a hot summer day. The projection of this however is very limited and can only be smelled nearby and barely leaves a scent trail.<br />
<br />
Scent: 6/10<br />
Performance: 6/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Sillage: 4/10<br />
Price: 7/10<br />

<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2095800">jaywizard</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-06">05/06/24 09:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I had to wear this on three separate occasions in order to form a somewhat comprehensible opinion about this fragrance here, Bleu de Chanel EDP. It's interesting as hell, because on the opening and out of the bottle, this smells absolutely so generic, just a clean soap/shower gel smell, with really nothing special to it. However,<br />
ehem,<br />
HOWEVER, once it dries, holy moly. This fragrance dries down into something elegant, complex and fresh with just a hint of spiciness. It resonates with the Chanel aesthetic and motif; seemingly simple on the outside yet meticulously engineered and designed within. It's difficult to imagine anyone disliking this scent once it is dried. It seems like the penultimate upper middle class dumb reach, since it could really work in any scenario, setting or season. Although it is quite expensive for a designer fragrance, and that is the one downside.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2147457"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2147457#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2146549" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2029669">TheFraganist55</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-01">05/01/24 07:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This stuff absolutely rocks. It's like the original BDC but deeper and creamier. You can wear it in any scenario or season. It is a masterpiece from opening to dry down. Opening is citrusy-fresh, and in the dry down it becomes creamy and smooth. I get 6-8 hours of longevity with ~2 hours of moderate projection. Not all fragrances need to have projection that covers half of a continent (I'm looking at you YSL Y EDP). BDC EDP has a comfortable projection that will make others want to be near you instead of push them away. Not to mention this fragrance is extremely masculine for a blue fragrance, probably because this is THE blue fragrance. Many blue frags have tried to emulate BDC, but none of them have been able to replicate the perfect balance of freshness, versatility, and masculinity that it provides.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; So this morning I wanted to pick a blue frag for work, and I was in between Imagination (too summery), Sedley (too light), and BdC EDP. BdC seemed the better pick because it has the spiciness added to the citrus to make it a little stronger - so I went with that. Later this morning, I am really enjoying this. Would be nice if it could just be appreciated for what it is without also having to fight past the stereotype of "nice, but basic and boring." It's really good, folks, in case you needed a reminder.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="2136928"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=2136928#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2136896" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2126593" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="cynogriffin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2038695"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="cynogriffin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Original-Penguin/Premium-Blend-38898.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.38898.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Premium Blend"title="Premium Blend"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2126593ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2126593" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2038695">cynogriffin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-16">04/16/24 12:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Good, fresh, all-around type fragrance, as others have said. Has a little more depth to it than your standard blue freshie. Maybe it was just the sample I had, but the performance was pretty not great on this one. Projected less than an hour and was gone in about 4-5 hours. Could just be me going nose-blind to it, but still pretty disappointing for an EDP, and one that costs a pretty penny at that. I personally think there are a lot of quality players in this space now in terms of DNA, and so it's less unique these days and has a lot more competition. It's not really a great value in terms of what you can get with a similar DNA at a better price point with better performance. Is it a good fragrance? Absolutely, it is quality and I think everyone should experience this DNA and know what BdC smells like because it is kind of an OG and set the standard for what a good blue fragrance can be. Is it worth getting? From what I have experienced and for me personally, not really. The amount I would have to spray on to get decent performance/projection out of it would just make it too expensive for what it is. I think there are a lot of other alternatives to consider out there.<br />
<br />
Good for those who want a people-pleaser and something that won't offend anyone and good for all occasions/seasons, but just know that you might have to invest a decent chunk of cash if you want to make it a signature or everyday fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; No one cares is a frag doesnt paint a picture for you...its to smell nice, not to take you away on a magical journey where virgin girls spritz aventus on you while baby angels poop nutella into a jar.<br />
<br />
EPD smells amazing, lasts 10+hrs on my skin and will be a bigger compliment getter than the original</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="567406"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=567406#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1499400" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If Bleu de Chanel has no fans, I no longer exist.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="1499400"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=1499400#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1139552" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1139552" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Erick B Easy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1192080"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1192080.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Erick B Easy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Prada/Prada-L-Homme-Intense-45396.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.45396.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Prada L'Homme Intense"title="Prada L'Homme Intense"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1139552ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1139552" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1192080">Erick B Easy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-01-29">01/29/20 17:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>There is a reason why this is so popular. Newsflash its really good. If you're not fully into fragrances and have no desire for a large collection and you just want something that smells really good and is super versatile this might be the one for you. Cold weather warm weather day or night work or play this will get the job done admirably at that. Better than YSL Y and Dior Sauvage imo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="1139552"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=1139552#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent605735" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc605735" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="olfactorium"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/726330"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.726330.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="olfactorium" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.607.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Allure Homme Sport"title="Allure Homme Sport"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma605735ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd605735" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/726330">olfactorium</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-06-20">06/20/15 15:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I suppose we can debate the merits of Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum until we are all “bleu” in the face and nothing will be resolved; nonetheless, I am here to tell you that Chanel does not make junk.  This company is a worldwide phenomenon and the owners, the Wertheimer brothers, have 6.3 billion reasons to maintain fastidious control over the quality and distribution of their products. Wearing Chanel fragrance, like wearing Chanel couture, is a mantle of discovery with many layers, often as incomprehensible as it is playful and alluring. That is called Chanel mystique.  You either get it or you don’t.  Whether this is due to Mr. Polge’s efforts alone or some other factors I can’t say, but it would be hard for anyone to believe that he could be creating fragrance after fragrance for more than thirty years if he did not possess a devilishly extraordinary (and monetarily successful) nose. <br />
<br />
If you think back to the origins of Chanel, you may remember that Coco Chanel not only freed women from corsetry, but made an art of mocking the very Edwardian prudes she converted, ladies who formerly rejected her in society until she made them all want to wear her little gray and navy uniforms. Decades later, when the Chanel look became dated, creative director, Karl Lagerfeld (who understood her divine contempt), was hired to revive the brand by producing unexpected, masterfully crafted, incomprehensible couture and the name “Chanel” once again ascended the worldwide stage.  Chanel is God.  Chanel is Satan.  Chanel is all the good and bad in all of us, and some of us hate it and others love, love, love it.  But if you think you are laughing at Chanel, please know there is a lot of cackling going on at 31 Rue Cambon, all the way to the Banque de France.<br />
<br />
Bleu de Chanel EDP is subject to all of the above.  You must pay the price to wear it, and wearing it is like wearing the whole history of the company with all of its strange idiosyncrasies and eccentricities.  Attempts to diminish Bleu de Chanel EDP by saying it smells like deodorant or some amalgam of chemicals are just naïve. Chanel pulled all its fragrances from drugstore shelves in the 1970’s to increase its luster and exclusivity. Beyond this, Chanel marketer Jean Hoene has been quoted as saying “We introduce a new fragrance every ten years, not every three minutes.”  It’s hard to imagine, with so much restraint and guile attributed to this brand, the House of Chanel would take the low road by releasing a trash fragrance.  Such a premise would be a non-sequitur anywhere those interlocking letters appear under license.<br />
<br />
There is no tidy way to describe Bleu de Chanel EDP, just as there is no tidy way to sum up the influence of Chanel on fashion.  The notes taken together seem to create something abstract or quixotic and the “professional” sample sniffers who promote enthusiasm for long extinct fragrances that have become fetid with the years and can only be purchased second hand are not qualified to critique Bleu de Chanel EDP, which is, in my opinion, pure modern luxury. There will never be another (1981) Chanel Antaeus, but there is good stuff in this flask. For example, if you bother to read the discreet embossing on the back of the box you will see that Bleu de Chanel EDP contains among its components extract of evernia prunastri or oakmoss (not listed in the pyramid above). Now restricted by IFRA, you will have to go far to find a comparably priced, recent release that contains the complex woody aroma of natural oakmoss. That’s just one of this deep blue bottle's little secrets.   <br />
<br />
Occasionally, I will write a negative review, but I haven’t made a life’s work out of it.  I would rather write about things which give me pleasure. The true irony here is that the “chemists”, on the other hand,  are often so intent on lampooning certain molecules they hate that they fail to recognize some of the better attars because their assumptions and egoism get in the way. However, if you keep an open mind (and you have established the funding) there are many things in life which hold delight:  I believe Bleu de Chanel EDP is not only one of them, but can‘t be anything less.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="605735"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=605735#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="25967" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc517354" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SimplyOliver"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/390452"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.390452.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SimplyOliver" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma517354ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd517354" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/390452">SimplyOliver</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-08-27">08/27/14 02:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Available in most French Sephos.<br />
<br />
Bleu EdP is basically a sweeter, toned down version of the original Bleu. I didn't get more woods, instead it seems that it's actually the amber notes that are more prominent than in the original, giving it a warmer feel. The citruses still play the main role, with the signature minty Bleu grapefruit. Overall the scent itself is in my opinion shallower than the original: very linear, just a more sugary Bleu with more amber, very little evolution. But it still retains the same clean and polite vibe as its predecessor. I was expecting more of a surprise, a bit more oomph, in the hope that Bleu could acquire a bit more depth. Not the case, sadly. <br />
Btw, the ashtray note has been 'removed' (I know some hated it), meaning that we're now left with an even more basic, sweet-citrus scent. The drydown is limited to a very cheap, synthetic amber. We're basically left wondering "that's it???".<br />
<br />
I also concur with other reviewers: performances are rather disappointing as well. Bleu EdP lasted 4-5 hours with average projection, when the EdT easily lasted 6 hours.<br />
<br />
As other have said before, it is rather luminous than dark, rather yellow than blue, rather... dull than unexpected: I even like the EdT better, which I feel is more complex, balanced, with better performances and overall better value for money (even though I don't praise it at all). <br />
<br />
Ladies and gentlemen, here is "the greatest parfum creation of the last 50 years" (source: Chanel marketing department). In the meantime, McDonald's has been awarded 3-star gastronomic restaurant by the Michelin guide. *chuckles*</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="517354"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=517354#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent535879" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
