padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc544385" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Coffee King"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/368581"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.368581.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Coffee King" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma544385ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd544385" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/368581">Coffee King</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-11-27">11/27/14 00:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Don't get the appeal at all, went in with hopes of it, came away with a bottle of Antaeus, what an absolutely dull and boring, generic fragrance.  Why can I not fall in love with Bleu in any of its formats, I wish I could smell what some of you guys are clearly seeing as a masterpiece.  Don't get it, 4/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="544385"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=544385#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent521860" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc521860" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fhr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/564540"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="fhr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Davidoff/Cool-Water-507.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.507.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Cool Water"title="Cool Water"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma521860ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd521860" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/564540">fhr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-09-11">09/11/14 04:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very disappointed with this EDP.Unfortunately because i had big expectations...<br />
I am a big fan of the EDT well balanced an pleasing from head-till-base notes. I do have that in my rotation since issued. <br />
But the ED:P head and middle notes are ok. But what comes after 30 mins I do not wish even for my enemies (good tahat i do not have none :-) )<br />
The base - what unfortunately stays on skin almost for a day and cannot be washed down - is the full chemically smelling artifical ambroxol,in an irritating and non pleasent way.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="25967"comment_id="521860"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Bleu-de-Chanel-Eau-de-Parfum-25967.html?ccid=521860#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="25967" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
